## minus one times surface upwelling shortwave flux in air
 PARSE: located_in(n(minus)-(n(one)-(n(times)-(n(surface)-(n(upwelling)-(n(shortwave)-n(flux)))))),material(n(air)))

## minus one times toa outgoing shortwave flux
 PARSE: term(minus one times toa outgoing shortwave flux)
 PARSE: n(minus)-(n(one)-(n(times)-term(toa outgoing shortwave flux)))
 PARSE: n(minus)-(n(one)-(n(times)-(n(toa)-(n(outgoing)-(n(shortwave)-n(flux))))))

## minus one times water flux into sea water from rivers
 PARSE: into(n(minus)-(n(one)-(n(times)-(n(water)-n(flux)))),material(n(sea)-(n(water)-(n(from)-n(rivers)))))

## model level number
 PARSE: term(model level number)
 PARSE: n(model)-(n(level)-n(number))

## model level number at base of ocean mixed layer defined by sigma theta
 PARSE: inheres_in(attribute(n(model)-(n(level)-(n(number)-(n(at)-n(base))))),n(ocean)-(n(mixed)-(n(layer)-(n(defined)-(n(by)-(n(sigma)-n(theta)))))))

## model level number at convective cloud base
 PARSE: term(model level number at convective cloud base)
 PARSE: n(model)-(n(level)-(n(number)-(n(at)-(n(convective)-(n(cloud)-n(base))))))

## model level number at convective cloud top
 PARSE: term(model level number at convective cloud top)
 PARSE: n(model)-(n(level)-(n(number)-(n(at)-(n(convective)-(n(cloud)-n(top))))))

## model level number at sea floor
 PARSE: term(model level number at sea floor)
 PARSE: n(model)-(n(level)-(n(number)-(n(at)-(n(sea)-n(floor)))))

## model level number at top of atmosphere boundary layer
 PARSE: inheres_in(attribute(n(model)-(n(level)-(n(number)-(n(at)-n(top))))),n(atmosphere)-(n(boundary)-n(layer)))

 PARSE: n(surface)-(n(snow)-(n(melt)-(n(heat)-n(flux))))

## surface snow sublimation amount
 PARSE: term(surface snow sublimation amount)
 PARSE: n(surface)-(n(snow)-(n(sublimation)-n(amount)))

## surface snow sublimation heat flux
 PARSE: term(surface snow sublimation heat flux)
 PARSE: n(surface)-(n(snow)-(n(sublimation)-(n(heat)-n(flux))))

## surface snow thickness
 PARSE: term(surface snow thickness)
 PARSE: n(surface)-(n(snow)-n(thickness))

## surface specific humidity
 PARSE: term(surface specific humidity)
 PARSE: n(surface)-term(specific humidity)
 PARSE: n(surface)-(n(specific)-n(humidity))

## surface temperature
 PARSE: term(surface temperature)
 PARSE: n(surface)-n(temperature)

## surface temperature anomaly
 PARSE: term(surface temperature anomaly)
 PARSE: n(surface)-(n(temperature)-n(anomaly))

## surface upward heat flux in air
 PARSE: located_in(n(surface)-(n(upward)-(n(heat)-n(flux))),material(n(air)))

## surface upward latent heat flux
 PARSE: term(surface upward latent heat flux)
 PARSE: n(surface)-(n(upward)-(n(latent)-(n(heat)-n(flux))))

## surface upward sensible heat flux
 PARSE: term(surface upward sensible heat flux)
 PARSE: n(surface)-(n(upward)-(n(sensible)-(n(heat)-n(flux))))

## surface upward water flux
 PARSE: term(surface upward water flux)
 PARSE: n(surface)-(n(upward)-(n(water)-n(flux)))

## surface upward water vapor flux in air
 PARSE: located_in(n(surface)-(n(upward)-(n(water)-(n(vapor)-n(flux)))),material(n(air)))

## surface upwelling longwave flux in air
 PARSE: located_in(n(surface)-(n(upwelling)-(n(longwave)-n(flux))),material(n(air)))

## surface upwelling longwave flux in air assuming clear sky
 PARSE: located_in(n(surface)-(n(upwelling)-(n(longwave)-n(flux))),material(n(air)-(n(assuming)-(n(clear)-n(sky)))))

## surface upwelling photosynthetic photon flux in air
 PARSE: located_in(n(surface)-(n(upwelling)-(n(photosynthetic)-(n(photon)-n(flux)))),material(n(air)))

## surface upwelling radiance in air
 PARSE: located_in(n(surface)-(n(upwelling)-n(radiance)),material(n(air)))

 PARSE: located_in(n(surface)-(n(upwelling)-n(radiance)),material(n(air)-(n(emerging)-(n(from)-(n(sea)-n(water))))))

 PARSE: located_in(n(surface)-(n(upwelling)-n(radiance)),material(n(air)-(n(reflected)-(n(by)-(n(sea)-n(water))))))

## surface upwelling radiance in sea water
 PARSE: located_in(n(surface)-(n(upwelling)-n(radiance)),material(n(sea)-n(water)))
